 Happy Holi 2019:phalgun shukla paksh kii poornima tithi par pradosh kaal main holikaa dahan kiya jaataa he
 According to astrology, Holi Dahan is considered superior during the Bhadra-free Pradosh period on Phalgun Purnima
 holikaa puja or dahan main parikrama behad mahatvapurn maani jaati he
 It is believed that if your wish is stated while circling, it comes true
 aisa bhi mana jaataa he ki holikaa dahan ke din safed khaadya padaarthon ke seven se bachanaa chahie
 Taking the remaining fire and ashes of Holi to your house in the morning the next day removes all the negative energy
 holikaa dahan kaa sahi muhoort-holikaa dahan muhoort-21:05 se 11:31 tak
 Bhadra Tail-17: 23 to 18:24
 bhadraa mukh-18:24 se 20:07 tak
 Rangwali Holi will be played on March 21
 poornima tithi aarambh-10:44 (20 march)poornima tithi samaapt-07:12 (21 march)kaise karen holikaa dahan-- holikaa dahan ke sthaan ko pehle gangaajal se shuddh karen
 - Place the Holika rung in the middle
 bhakt prahlada kaa pratik ek danda hota he
 - Put sandal wood first around the poles
 - iske baad saamaanya lakadiyaan, upale or ghaas chadhayen
 - Light a fire with camphor - In Holika Dahan, first worship Shri Ganesh Hanuman ji and Sheetla Mata Bhairav ji
 - agni main roli, pushp, chaaval, saabut mung, hare chane, papad, nariyal aadi chijen chadhayen
 - Keep dry fruits, dry wood, dry grass all around
 iske baad agni jalaaen or holikaa dahan karen
 - Mantra - Prahladeye Namah, do the circumambulation by speaking
 holikaa kii agni main kya arpit karen-- achche swasthya ke liye-holikaa kii agni menkale til ke dane arpit karen
 - To get rid of the disease- Offer green cardamom and camphor
 - dhan laabh ke liye- chandan kii lakdi arpit karen
 - For employment - Offer yellow mustard
 - vivaah or vaivaahik samasyaon ke liye-havan saamagree arpit karen
 - To get rid of negative energy - Offer black mustard
 holikaa dahan kii parampara-bhartiya nav sanvatsar caitra shukla pratipada kii pehali tithi ko shuru hota he
 Before its arrival, the old Samvatsara is said to farewell
 puraane samvath ko samaapt karne ke liye holikaa dahan kiya jaataa he
 It is also called burning of Samvat
 holikaa dahan main kisi vriksh ki shakha ko jameen ke andar daalaa jaataa he, chaaron taraf se lakadiyaan, upalon se gher kar nishchit muhoort main jalaayaa jaataa he
 In this, dung cakes, new wheat earrings and herbs are burnt, so that a person can get health throughout the year, and all his evil abuses are consumed in the fire
 kai jagahon par holikaa dahan ke baad uski raakh ko ghar main laakar usase tilak karne kii parampara bhi he
 Story of Holika Dahan - Hiranyakashipu's son Prahlada was a devotee of Lord Vishnu
 lekin hiranyakashiphu bhagwaan vishnu kaa ghor virdohi tha
 Hiranyakashipu tried several times to kill Prahlada
 kaha jaataa he usne prahlada ko maarane ke liye bahan holikaa kaa sahaara liya tha
 Holika got the boon of not burning in the fire, so Holika sat in the fire with Prahlad
 lekin shri vishnu ne prahlaad kii raksha kii or holikaa aagni main bhasma ho gai
 Since then, the practice of Holika Dahan started
 holikaa dahan ke laabh-- is din man kii tamaam samasyaon kaa nivaaran ho saktaa he
 The problem of many diseases and opponents can be overcome
 - aarthik baadhaon se raahat mil sakati he
 - One can easily get the blessings of God on this day
 - alag-alag chizon ko agni main daalkar apni baadhaon se mukti paa sakate hai

 jinhen rashtrawaad shabd se dikkat he unhen patrkaar kaise kah sakate hai, jabaki sachai yahi he ki jab kahin kisi kii baat nahin suni jaati to vah media ke daravaaje par aata he

 GST means India's biggest tax reform will not be monitored by the Constitutional Auditor General and Auditor General (CAG)! If Parliament does not interfere, the CAG will not be able to question the loss of benefits to the Center and states from GST! ambedkar ne kaha tha ki sieji supreme court se zyada mahatvapurn sanstha he
 It has the constitutional right to certify the revenue of the Center and the states, but it will not get the right to ask for information regarding revenue in GST
 rajya sarkarein bhi kab chaahati hai ki koi unki nigaraanee kare
 Is it a fear of the cag's activism in the previous government? Or is there a big event to limit the role of constitutional bodies? GST deals with the revenue of governments (central and state), which are part of the constitutional rules of audit
 isi aadhaar par sieji ne 2ji or koyala ghotaalon kii jaanch kii thi, kyonki unase mila rajasav sarkari khajaane main aayaa tha
 Under Section 65 of the preliminary draft of the GST Act, the CAG was empowered to call for information from the GST Council
 pichley saal aktubar main, centre sarkaar ke netritv main chupchaap is praavdhaan ko hataane kii kavayad shuru hui
 The CAG wrote a letter requesting that Section 65 should not be removed as it is the responsibility of the CAG to audit the tax matters of the constitutional rules
 alabatta jiesti council kii taaja baithak main centre or rajya sieji ko jiesti se dur rakhane par raji ho gaye
 After this decision, the role of the constitutional auditor in the revenue of the Center and states will be very limited
 sarkarein jiesti se sieji ko kyon dur rakhana chaahati hai, is par shaq lajimi he

 is samay bhi halaat kuch aise hi hai

 kii bachat ke daawey ko khokhla sabit kiya tha

 The jury that selected the winners for the Booker Prize this year broke the rules and declared Margaret Atwood and Bernardine Everisto the joint winners for the award
 evaristo is pratishthit puraskaar ko jeetne vaali pehali ashwet mahila hai
 The six books shortlisted for the award included british-indian novelist Salman Rushdie's novel "quichote"
 bukar ke niyamon ke anusaar is puraskaar ko baanta nahin ja saktaa, lekin nirnaayak mandal ne kaha ki ve atwood ke ‘da testament' or evaristo ke ‘girl, vuman, adar' main se kisi ek ko nahin chun sakate
 These awards were instituted in 1969
 isse pehle 1992 main do logon ko sanyukt rup se yah puraskaar diya gaya tha
 After this the rules were changed
 aayojakon ne is saal ke nirnaayak mandal se kaha tha ki ve do vijetaon ko nahin chun sakate

 to mujhe thodaa sankoch hota
